Aisa bhi toh ni h na yrr ke maine kbhi tujhe apne way mai badalne ka try na koya ho smjhaya naa ho arw badlne ka chor maine toh tujhe saari conditions bhi btayi h....har ek baar har ek moment pe....tu ni ban skti h bey waise....tu apne ko aap ko jaise strting mai thi waisa hi h...jab hum bestfriends the khch ni bdla h aaj tk tere mai....tu bhi janti h har din kitta khch chlta raeh raa h meri life mai aaj kl har cheej se alag way mai jaa raa hui r sab cheejen mere oppose mai.....itna sab hone pe obvious h na yrr ke har ek cheej express out krne ke liye ek person ki want rkh skun.....
Arsh se sab btata hui cause woh uss way se btati h bolti h smjhati h smjhti h...jo bhi h bla blaa.....
Taise bhi maine yee cheej btayi h naa har baar kitte baar tujhe smjhane ka try Kiya h maine....Abey yr tu hi bta roj roj itte saare cheejon se deal out krke aari hogi tu tujhe ek person ki need nhi hogi kya jisse tu aake reliefly sb bta ske jo tu apne partner se nhi kr skti.....
Mai Taiko uss way mai treat krta hui har ek baar jab tu khch btati iss liye tera mind ni jata kisi r person ke taraf.....tu ni h uss tarah iss liye mera jata h.....
R maine even tho usse tk itta btaya h agar mai kbhi Taiko chor duin toh please arsh tu usse heal kriyo har uss way mai jis way mai tum dono ke worst phase mai tha.....
R Taiko lgta h ke mai usko Terese jyda prioritise krta hui.....
Abey Arohii tu bhi toh soch na bey long distance mai bs online friends h hum dono tujhe har baar lgta h ke mai Taiko chor ke usse date krne lgunga.....chutiya h kya bey dost h bs woh meri are bhai ab toh woh bhi aa gyi h relationship Mai ab kaise proof krun mai.....
5 din sb khch btaunga as like it is fir khch din baad Mera man ni krega btane ko cause uss way mai treatment ni milegi jis way mai genuinely koi person chahta h ke usse treat Kiya jaaye uss specific moment uss specific cheej ke liye.....fir whi hoga mental health ki aisi ki taisi ho jayegi wAise bhi hui pri h...r jyda ho jayegi....fir relationship r khrb hoga pta h maiko experience kr chuka hui ye cheej.....

R upar se sbko saath leke ni chl skte Abey mai ghnta ni chlna chahta Hui sbko saath leke alag alag place pe ho dono alag alag values hold krte ho.....arey mai bhi janta Hui ni rhta h khch saath hmesha konsa mai bol raa maiko woh apne pure life mai chahiye.....Abey ek state mai bhi nahi h humlog online way mai bs connected h kaise mai hope krlun ke ek gf hone ke bawjud mai usse forever hold kr paunga......Abey khch saal ki baat h bey khch saal mai uski bhi shaadi ho jayegi meri bhi alag ho jayenge dono baat tk ni ho payegi fir....future mai dono ko pta h ke alag ho jayenge..... kyunki humlog sirf bestfriends h girlfriend r boyfriend nahi.....
Thik h woh agar hum dono ke bich Mai ghusti agar tb mai bolta na Kahan kbhi kiya h usne ye cheej aaj tk....never ever....Abey usse bhi pta h yrr uski limits Kahan tk h r Kahan nhi.....tune hi khud bola tha na abhi Arohii ke maise uski baat Mt Kriyo aaj ke baad.....usne toh aaj tk ni bola na.....even kayi baar ussne btaya maiko guide Kiya h kis way mai hum dono apni ldayi khtm kr skte h....ekdam acche se sb smjhti h jab bhi khch btata usse tere baare mai.....mai toh ye bhi ni bol raa naa yr ke tu uski saari baat sun merese jo mai btaun uske baare mai...khud ni btata ab mai....bich Mai bs bht chinta ho rhi thi ke kya hua hoga kyun badal gyi woh iss liye btaya taise....iss liye ni btaya tha ke tu uski baate sune mujhe bilkul accha feel nahi ho raha tha iss liye btaya taise taki thora normal lge ke tu thora comfort kre....tu ulta oppose krne lg gyi jati h.....Abey ab toh thik h ni bta raa khch bhi uske baare mai Taiko.....ye kya hmesha compare krte rhti h khud ko usse woh better h ye cheej h woh cheej h...nahi h khch aisa bolta hui taise khch smjh hi ni aata Taiko...hmesha ek hi cheej hi kaheti dimag nhi khrb hoga kya fir......


Ek cheej boli thi bs ke please insta I'd mat htaiyo.....iss liye nhi ke apni baat ni hogi insta pe iss liye cause strting se apne bond ka sb connection se lekar har ek cheej insta pe hi Hui h.....ek cheej bs boli thi taise usmai bhi tu ni smjhi.....aisa ni h ke ye bhi ni smjhaya arey itta smjhata hui taiko har ek cheej ke liye pta nahir kaise btaun r kya btaun.....ke tujhe smjh aa jaye har baar baat ke prespective ki nahi alag alag viewpoint ki hoti h....maine toh haar baar tujhe sb smjhaya h koi bhi ek topic nikal lee mai surety deta Hui aisa ho hi ni skta ke maine Taiko uss cheej ke liye 1 se kam baar smjhaya ho.....are hazaron baar ek cheej btayi h taiko taaki tu bhi smjhe ke kya reality r kya ek human need hoti h jo aapka partner aapse chahta h but ni milti h toh dusre se whi sab cheej btata.....r agar aisa ho toh bs usse har cheej se disappointment r failures milte just because usne dono person ko kbhi bhi ek baar bhi hurt nhi karna chaha!!....
